. // Temperature rise deemed acceptable
. * Binary variable being 1 if temperature rise above 1.5 degrees i
> s deemed acceptable and 0 otherwise
. gen temp_above = .
(277 missing values generated)

. replace temp_above = 0 if temp_rise <= 1.5
(216 real changes made)

. replace temp_above = 1 if temp_rise > 1.5
(61 real changes made)

. lab var temp_above "Temperature rise above 1.5°C deemed acceptabl
> e"

. do "C:\Users\MAXBUR~1\AppData\Local\Temp\STD25c8_000000.tmp"

. 
. * Cropped temperature rise deemed acceptable
. /*
> Very few people suggested temperatures of 2.5°C or higher to be a
> cceptable:
> 2.5°C -> 9
> 3.0°C -> 4
> 3.5°C -> 2
> 4.0°C -> 2
> 4.5°C -> 0
> 5.0°C -> 4
> Therefore, for the illustration Figure 1a all temperature suggest
> ions of 2.5°C or more are summarized under >= 2.5°C
> */
. gen temp_rise2 = temp_rise

. replace temp_rise2 = 2.5 if temp_rise >= 2.5
(12 real changes made)

. tostring temp_rise2, gen(temp_rise3)
temp_rise3 generated as str3

. sort temp_rise

. lab define temp 1 "0" 2 ".5" 3 "1" 4 "1.5", replace

. encode temp_rise3, gen(temp_rise_cropped) lab(temp)

. lab var temp_rise_cropped"All those suggesting 2.5 or more collec
> ted in 2.5"

. drop temp_rise2 temp_rise3

. 
. 
end of do-file

. do "C:\Users\MAXBUR~1\AppData\Local\Temp\STD25c8_000000.tmp"

. 
. 
. /*
> Carbon price suggestions tested
> Different models suggest different minimal global carbon prices t
> o stay below a certain temperature rise. In the main paper we use
>  USD60 as thte threshold. As robustness test, we also test agains
> t other specifications: 37 USD 82 USD, 185 USD, 281 USD
> */
. foreach i in 37 60 82 185 281 {
  2.         gen price_below_`i' = .
  3.                 replace price_below_`i'= 1 if carbon_price < `
> i'
  4.                 replace price_below_`i'= 0 if carbon_price >= 
>  `i'
  5.         lab var price_below_`i' "Price below USD `i' suggested
> "
  6. }

> s 50 USD [...]"

> SD) as appropriate"

>  three low temperature options (0°C, 0.5°C and 1°C), with price s
> uggestions ranging from 0 to 2,000 USD (Levene’s test F(1, 275)=2
> 1.7, p<0.001)."

. ** Global carbon price and temperature rise 
. * Global Generate variable defining position of observations on x
> -axis
. egen carbon_price_rank = rank(carbon_price_cap), by(temp_rise_cro
> pped) unique

. egen temp_rise_cropped_freq = count(carbon_price_cap), by(temp_ri
> se_cropped)

. gen  temp_rise_cropped_jitter2 = temp_rise_cropped + (carbon_pric
> e_rank *.006) - (temp_rise_cropped_freq / 2 * 0.006)

. 
. * National: Generate variable defining position of observations o
> n x-axis
. foreach var in now future {
  2. egen price_rank_h_`var' = rank(price_home_`var'_cap), unique
  3. }

. 
. gen h_now_jitter = .
(276 missing values generated)

. replace h_now_jitter = .5 + (price_rank_h_now *.001)
(276 real changes made)

. gen h_future_jitter = .
(276 missing values generated)

. replace h_future_jitter = 1 + (price_rank_h_future * .001)
(276 real changes made)

. gen h_now_stat = .
(276 missing values generated)

. replace h_now_stat = .6
(276 real changes made)

. gen h_future_stat = .
(276 missing values generated)

. replace h_future_stat = 1.1
(276 real changes made)

. // Temperature rise deemed acceptable

> therwise
. gen temp_above = .
(277 missing values generated)

. replace temp_above = 0 if temp_rise <= 1.5
(216 real changes made)

. replace temp_above = 1 if temp_rise > 1.5
(61 real changes made)

. lab var temp_above "Temperature rise above 1.5°C deemed acceptable"

. 
. * Cropped temperature rise deemed acceptable
. /*
> Very few people suggested temperatures of 2.5°C or higher to be acceptable:
> 2.5°C -> 9
> 3.0°C -> 4
> 3.5°C -> 2
> 4.0°C -> 2
> 4.5°C -> 0
> 5.0°C -> 4
> Therefore, for the illustration Figure 1a all temperature suggestions of 2.5°C or more are s
> ummarized under >= 2.5°C
> */
. gen temp_rise2 = temp_rise

. replace temp_rise2 = 2.5 if temp_rise >= 2.5
(12 real changes made)

. tostring temp_rise2, gen(temp_rise3)
temp_rise3 generated as str3

. sort temp_rise

. lab define temp 1 "0" 2 ".5" 3 "1" 4 "1.5", replace

. encode temp_rise3, gen(temp_rise_cropped) lab(temp)

. lab var temp_rise_cropped"All those suggesting 2.5 or more collected in 2.5"

. drop temp_rise2 temp_rise3

. // Global carbon price suggested

. replace carbon_price_cap  = 501 if carbon_price > 500

. egen median_carbon_price = median(carbon_price), by(temp_rise_cropped)

. lab var median_carbon_price "Median carbon price (non-capped)"

. * Global Generate variable defining position of observations on x-axis

> cropped_freq / 2 * 0.006)

  3. }

(277 missing values generated)

. replace h_now_jitter = .5 + (price_rank_h_now *.001)
(277 real changes made)

. gen h_future_jitter = .
(277 missing values generated)

. replace h_future_jitter = 1 + (price_rank_h_future * .001)
(277 real changes made)

. gen h_now_stat = .
(277 missing values generated)

. replace h_now_stat = .6
(277 real changes made)

. * Global Generate variable defining position of observations on x-axis

> cropped_freq / 2 * 0.006)

  3. }

(277 missing values generated)

(277 real changes made)

(277 missing values generated)

. replace h_future_jitter = 1 + (price_rank_h_future * .001)
(277 real changes made)

(277 missing values generated)

. replace h_now_stat = .6
(277 real changes made)
